![城市街头肖像与卡通内在自我二人组](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143613840_3ofbkw_G-MH5fIbMAAmHyw.jpg)

```
Transform this image [Upload Your Image] into a 64K DSLR shot resolution of A creative urban street portrait featuring a young man (same face as the uploaded image) sitting on a curb in a quiet city street, paired with a stylized cartoon illustration of himself placed beside him. The real-life subject (same face as the uploaded image) is seated casually on a concrete sidewalk edge, resting his head on one hand in a bored, contemplative pose. He looks slightly upward with a neutral, introspective expression, conveying a sense of quiet thoughtfulness and urban solitude. He wears a muted maroon cable-knit sweater with a relaxed fit, dark loose-fitting denim jeans with subtle stitched details near the cuffs, and worn brown leather boots. Accessories include layered silver chain dog tag with the name "{argument name="dog tag text" default="[Add Text]"}" written on it, rings on his fingers, black-framed glasses, and a light-coloured baseball cap with bold embroidered lettering on the front. His hair is short, dark hair, a well-groomed beard texture and character. Next to him on the sidewalk sits a small cartoon version (same face as the uploaded image) of himself, matching his outfit and pose exactly—same sweater, jeans, boots, cap, glasses, and facial expression. The illustrated character has clean outlines, warm muted colors, and a soft shaded, hand-drawn animation style, creating a playful contrast between realism and illustration. The cartoon figure is proportionally smaller, emphasizing a companion-like or inner-self concept. The background features textured cobblestone pavement, a curb edge, and a building facade with muted yellow walls and green-tiled brickwork near a window. The color palette is earthy and subdued, with natural daylight providing soft, even lighting and realistic shadows. The overall composition blends street photography, fashion portraiture, and mixed-media digital art, evoking themes of identity, self-reflection, and creativity.
Style & Mood Keywords: Urban street photography, casual fashion portrait, mixed media art, real and cartoon character duo, introspective mood, muted earthy tones, soft natural light, realistic textures, creative storytelling, high-resolution detail, cinematic realism. Octane render & Unreal Engine
```

```
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",

    },

      "orientation": "portrait",
```

### 10. 电影感街头时尚编辑肖像

### 19. Photorealistic Surreal Fashion Concept Portrait with Identity Lock

**Author**: [Özge](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> An extremely detailed, structured prompt for Nano Banana Pro focused on replicating a specific surreal fashion concept from a reference image. The core concept is an illusion where an open magazine held in front of the face perfectly replaces the subject's face with the printed model's face, including a seamless 'hair extension' column. It mandates strict identity lock and ultra-photoreal editorial style.

![Photorealistic Surreal Fashion Concept Portrait with Identity Lock](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508465813_ew0ftn_G9rQw0SX0AEHqSI.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_surreal_fashion_concept_portrait",
      "version": "v3.2_MAGAZINE_FLIP_HAIR_ILLUSION_EDITORIAL_IDENTITY_LOCK",
      "priority": "highest"
    },
    "references": {
      "reference_image_1": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE (REQUIRED)",
        "purpose": "COMPOSITION_AND_PROP_CONCEPT_LOCK + IDENTITY_LOCK",
        "strict_identity_lock": true,
        "face_match_strength": "max",
        "no_identity_drift": true,
        "preserve_unique_features": true,
        "preserve_skin_tone": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true
      }
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "ultra_photoreal_high_fashion_editorial",
      "sharpness": "crisp_but_natural",
      "film_grain": "none_or_minimal",
      "color_grade": "clean_editorial_neutral_luxury"
    },
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "ULTRA-PHOTOREAL HIGH-FASHION CONCEPT PORTRAIT — MUST MATCH THE UPLOADED REFERENCE IMAGE 100%.\n\nRecreate the exact same concept, pose, framing, and composition as the reference: a person stands indoors holding an open fashion magazine vertically in front of their face. The alignment is perfect so the printed model’s face in the magazine becomes the person’s face (illusion must be seamless). The printed hair continues upward into the top page as a long, clean, straight vertical hair strip, forming a surreal 'hair extension' column.\n\nIDENTITY REQUIREMENTS:\n- The person must be an exact, perfect match to the uploaded reference (no changes to facial structure, eyes, nose, lips, brows, proportions, ethnicity, age, skin tone).\n- Preserve all unique facial details and natural skin texture (pores, tiny imperfections). No beautification that changes identity.\n\nKEY ILLUSION DETAILS (MATCH REFERENCE):\n- Magazine open and held high with one hand above the head, pages extended vertically.\n- Printed beauty portrait shows pastel/lilac eye makeup and a neutral expression.\n- Hair strip: long vertical section with subtle gradient (darker near scalp, lighter at tips), clean and graphic.\n- Clothing: oversized textured knit sweater in warm autumn tones (rust/orange with subtle pattern), long cozy sleeves.\n- Paper realism: visible thickness, page curl, sharp edges, realistic print texture.\n\nENVIRONMENT (MATCH REFERENCE):\nMinimal indoor background with soft daylight, neutral walls, subtle architectural/window lines. Clean, uncluttered.\n\nLIGHTING & REALISM:\nSoft natural daylight, realistic shadows from magazine onto sweater and background. Knit fabric and paper texture must be crisp. > A collection of three highly detailed, cinematic prompts for generating photorealistic couple portraits, all requiring reference images for identity matching. The scenarios include a romantic kiss on an ancient stone balcony, a serene moment on a tropical beach at golden hour, and an Indian wedding portrait under a chandelier.
```

![Couple Portrait Prompts (Indian Wedding, Tropical Beach)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508446909_0nclxy_G9o8vW3a4AAKIkI.jpg)
![Couple Portrait Prompts (Indian Wedding, Tropical Beach)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508447894_atp7ph_G9o8vX3aMAsyOCT.jpg)
![Couple Portrait Prompts (Indian Wedding, Tropical Beach)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508448643_wpgvhd_G9o8vZhaMAsjPLN.jpg)
![Couple Portrait Prompts (Indian Wedding, Tropical Beach)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508449189_kts9tj_G9o8vaKaMAE-c6I.jpg)

```
Prompt 1:
"High-impact cinematic depiction of male from reference image(match face), featuring a sharp jawline, light stubble, and a gentle expression, with wavy dark hair, wearing a black and white patterned button-down shirt and round dark sunglasses. He is leaning in for a kiss with female from reference image(match face), who has long dark wavy hair with red highlights and subtle gold earrings, dressed in a vibrant {argument name="saree color" default="yellow"} embroidered traditional saree. Positioned in a sun-drenched ancient stone balcony with ornate arches, surrounded by blooming pink bougainvillea. The scene conveys romance and intimacy through warm golden hour natural lighting, with soft rim light on their hair. Captured using a 50mm lens, shallow depth of field with a blurred architectural background, cinematic framing. Ultra-detailed textures, realistic skin tones, professional cinematic color grading, sharp focus, HDR, ultra-high resolution, 4K, masterpiece quality."

Prompt 2:
```

### 36. Unfiltered Smartphone Photo of Man in Shopping Cart in Liquor Store

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-01-01  **Language**: en

> An extremely detailed prompt designed to generate an unfiltered, imperfect smartphone photo (RAW look) of a man sitting in a shopping cart inside a narrow liquor store aisle. The prompt enforces an absolute face lock from a reference image and mandates awkwardness, clutter, and visual noise, explicitly forbidding beautification, cinematic lighting, or product advertising aesthetics.

![Unfiltered Smartphone Photo of Man in Shopping Cart in Liquor Store](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508383844_j9ww0m_G9kGS_PbIAAVhu2.jpg)

```
FACE LOCK (MANDATORY):
Use the exact same face from the uploaded reference image with absolutely no modification. Facial structure, proportions, bone shape, eyes, nose, mouth, jawline, skin tone, pores, micro-texture, age, and identity must remain 100% identical. No beautification, no smoothing, no glow, no expression enhancement. Hair must remain exactly the same as in the reference image.

LOCATION:
Indoor liquor store aisle. Both sides of the frame are tightly packed with shelves of alcohol bottles (whisky, rum, cognac). Glass bottles with colorful labels, handwritten white price numbers on shelf edges. Warm yellow store lighting. Narrow aisle, crowded and visually noisy environment.

SUBJECT:
One adult man with a lean athletic build, clean-shaven, natural human proportions, real skin texture with visible pores and imperfections.

POSE (LOCKED — MUST MATCH REFERENCE IMAGE 1 EXACTLY):
The man is sitting inside a standard metal shopping cart, body reclined backward inside the cart (not upright). Both legs extended forward toward the camera, one leg slightly higher than the other, the sole of one shoe clearly facing the camera. Back resting against the rear of the cart. One arm resting casually along the side of the cart. Head turned slightly to the side (not facing the camera). Facial expression relaxed, careless, unaware of being photographed. Do not adjust the pose for the location.

PROP:
One expensive alcohol bottle held loosely in one hand, resting naturally near his thigh or hip. Not lifted, not centered, not presented. Brand name unreadable and not emphasized. Bottle feels heavy and real, not decorative.

OUTFIT:
{argument name="jacket color" default="Red"} racing-style jacket worn casually, dark denim jeans with natural creases, dark shoes with visibly worn soles, black sunglasses worn indoors without intention. Clothing looks worn, unplanned, and accidental — not styled.

LIGHTING:
Warm overhead liquor-store lighting. Flat exposure, minimal shadow depth. No cinematic lighting, no spotlight, no HDR, no glow.

CAMERA & FRAMING:
Shot on iPhone, RAW look. Vertical 9:16. Wide-lens perspective with slight natural distortion from the narrow aisle. Eye-level to slightly low angle. Handheld feel with imperfect framing. Slight grain and imperfect sharpness like a real phone photo.

REALISM RULES:
Do not beautify the subject. Do not improve posture. Do not stylize the environment. Do not turn the bottle into a hero product. Allow awkwardness, clutter, visual noise, and imperfection.

NEGATIVE PROMPT:
AI-generated look, CGI, 3D render, editorial fashion shoot, cinematic lighting, HDR, glow, plastic or waxy skin, beauty filter, over-sharpening, perfect symmetry, product advertising pose, readable brand logos, distorted anatomy, extra limbs, floating objects, watermark.
```

```
- Frame 1: wearing a sparkly "{argument name="year crown" default="2026"}" crown, smiling

- Frame 4: making peace signs, excited expression

- No other people visible
- No logos, watermarks, or UI elements
- No numbers outside the print strip
- Person appears ONLY inside the printed photos
Face Consistency Lock: The facial structure, eye spacing, nose bridge, jawline, and all identifying features must match the reference with 100% accuracy across all 4 frames. @AdobeFirefly
```

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张逼真的、电影级的、复古风格的彩色照片，内容是一位年轻女性骑着一辆 {argument name="motorcycle model" default="黑色 Royal Enfield Bullet 350"}。它严格要求 100% 保留参考图像中的面部特征，并包含服装、运动模糊和色彩分级的具体细节。

```
  "style": "photorealistic, cinematic, vintage-inspired color photography",

    "use_reference_image": true,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,

  },

    "gender": "female",
    "age_group": "young adult",
    "height": "5'7",
    "build": "slim-fit",
    "action": "riding a motorcycle",
    "pose": {
      "body_position": "leaning naturally into the ride",
      "hands": "both hands on the handlebars",
      "head_direction": "glancing confidently to the side"
    },
    "appearance": {
      "wardrobe": {
        "top": "oversized white linen shirt with top buttons open",
        "bottoms": "light blue baggy jeans",
        "footwear": "clean white Nike Air Force 1 sneakers"
      },
      "accessories": [
        "silver wristwatch",
        "narrow-frame rectangular classy sunglasses"
      ],
      "face_visibility": "fully visible"
    }
  },
  "vehicle": {
    "type": "motorcycle",
    "model": "{argument name="motorcycle model" default="black Royal Enfield Bullet 350"}"
  },
  "environment": {
    "setting": "open road",
    "atmosphere": "dynamic and confident riding moment"
  },
  "lighting": {

    "effect": [
      "realistic highlights on skin and fabric",
      "subtle reflections on motorcycle and watch"
    ]
  },
  "camera": {

    "motion_effect": "subtle motion blur to convey speed",

  },
  "color_grading": {
    "palette": "natural yet cinematic colors",
    "contrast": "moderate",

    "notes": "Maintain rich color tones instead of black-and-white while preserving a cinematic vintage feel."
  },

    "atmosphere": "confident, free-spirited, cinematic",
```

### 67. 图像到图像风格迁移：碎石雕塑

**Author**: [Dr.duet](https://x.com/Sheldon056)  **Date**: 2025-12-28  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的图像到图像风格迁移提示，指示 AI 将输入图像的主体重新创建为超现实的 3D 碎石组合（板岩和砂岩碎片），强调分离的碎片、凿刻的边缘、影棚灯光，并严格保留主体的身份和轮廓。

![图像到图像风格迁移：碎石雕塑](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061744152_69s9uv_G9OaElubgAAnxxj.jpg)
![图像到图像风格迁移：碎石雕塑](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061744011_cjdhy0_G9OaEllbgAAqrdQ.jpg)
![图像到图像风格迁移：碎石雕塑](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061744144_ae1fng_G9OaElvaMAAp0Wk.jpg)
![图像到图像风格迁移：碎石雕塑](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767061746571_zy37xw_G9OaEmbbQAAkchO.jpg)

```
task": "image_to_image_style_transfer",
  "input_image": "{{USER_IMAGE}}",
  "prompt": "Create a hyper-real 3D studio composition that recreates the main subject from the provided image as a fragmented stone assemblage. The subject must be built from separate, clearly detached rock pieces with small visible gaps between shards (no pieces merging). Material look: fragmented {argument name="stone type" default="slate + sandstone"} shards with chiseled edges, crisp fractures, visible stone grain, micro-scratches, and realistic roughness. Color palette: predominantly dark slate with subtle warm-ochre sandstone accents. Lighting: soft studio key light from top-left, gentle fill, subtle contact shadows under each shard, realistic ambient occlusion in crevices, clean reflections kept minimal. Background: minimal off-white seamless backdrop, no texture. Framing: centered, clean, straight-on, subject fully readable. Add a few tiny debris chips floating or resting near the base for depth. Preserve the subject’s identity, proportions, and recognizable silhouette from the input image while transforming all surfaces into stone fragments. Hyper-real, high detail, sharp focus, 8k render quality.",
  "negative_prompt": "text, typography, logo, watermark, signature, extra props, busy background, fog, heavy bloom, cartoon, illustration, lowpoly, plastic, metal, glossy paint, melted shapes, merged fragments, unreadable subject, blur, noise, low resolution, oversharpening halos, distorted face/body, extra limbs, deformed geometry",
  "output": {
    "aspect_ratio": "use_input_aspect_ratio",
    "background": "off_white",
    "camera": {
      "angle": "straight_on",
      "framing": "centered",
      "distance": "medium"
    }
  },
  "params": {
    "style_strength": 0.75,
    "identity_preservation": 0.9,
    "detail_level": "very_high",
    "lighting_preset": "soft_studio_top_left",
    "shadow_intensity": "subtle",
    "gap_visibility": "clear",
    "debris_chips": "few_tiny",
    "no_text": true
  }
}
```

```
  },
```

```
  },

  "appearance": {
    "hair": "Dark brown or black bob with bangs.",
    "makeup": "Vibrant red lipstick and defined eyeliner, visible only inside the focused rectangle.",

    "expression": "Neutral, direct gaze."
  },

  "environment": {
    "type": "Outdoor Seaside",
    "details": "Open sea background with a clean horizon line, softly blurred, natural coastal atmosphere."
  },

    "style": "Split / Composite",
    "focused_area": "Bright, clean natural light on the eye inside the rectangle.",
    "blurred_area": "Soft, diffused ambient light.",
    "shadows": "Minimal shadows in the focused area, undefined in the blurred regions."
  },

  "camera_shot": {
    "shot_type": "Medium Close-Up",
    "angle": "Eye-level, straight-on",
    "lens": "Sharp area simulates a 50mm or 85mm lens; blurred areas simulate extreme shallow depth of field or digital blur.",
    "focus": "Extreme selective focus. A vertical rectangular frame aligned over the woman's left eye is perfectly sharp, everything outside is heavily blurred."
  },

  "style": {
    "genre": "Experimental Editorial Fashion / Graphic Design",
    "mood": "Minimalist, modern, mysterious, sophisticated",
    "color_palette": {
      "primary": "Natural seaside blues",
      "secondary": "Skin tones",
```

### 74. 超逼真冬季肖像序列，带身份锁定

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，指示模型在生成一个三帧、超写实的冬季肖像序列时，要保持与参考图像绝对一致的面部身份，该序列设定在白雪覆盖的公园的蓝色时刻，强调分子级别的纹理细节和精确的大气渲染。

![超逼真冬季肖像序列，带身份锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987693469_oy30vs_G9LurXDaAAA_qIL.jpg)

**Author**: [Dr.duet](https://x.com/Sheldon056)  **Date**: 2025-12-27  **Language**: en

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 模型提供一个高度详细的提示，以生成一张超真实、电影级的时尚编辑照片。照片中，一名年轻男子在金色时段骑着一只巨大的柔和蓝色鸟，置身于广阔的野花田中，并严格指示模型精确保留上传的参考面部。

![电影级编辑奇幻肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987710983_mtpkdo_G9LVIRXawAAdnGQ.jpg)

```
Create a cinematic ultra-real editorial fashion photograph using my uploaded reference image. DO NOT CHANGE THE FACE.
The young man’s face must remain 100% identical to the reference — same facial structure, proportions, expression, and identity.

SKIN & REALISM

Ultra-real human skin with even tone and natural micro-variation. Visible pores, fine lines, tiny imperfections, and a subtle daylight sheen only.
Absolutely NO blush, no beauty filter, no plastic smoothing, no CGI look, no oversharpening.

SCENE & PROPS

A vast wildflower field filled with pink, lilac, and butter-yellow blooms, stretching toward low rolling hills beneath a big, clean open sky.
A giant pastel-blue bird with layered, slightly iridescent feathers. The bird wears slender reins and a simple dark saddle — minimal, realistic, no logos, no text, no branding.
Foreground flowers create soft natural bokeh, with a few drifting petals near the lens for depth and atmosphere.

WARDROBE (MODERN, MINIMAL, STREETWEAR)

A clean, premium oversized modern T-shirt in soft off-white or muted neutral tone, structured yet relaxed, matte fabric with natural folds.
Baggy straight-leg jeans, high-quality denim in washed light blue or soft grey, sitting naturally on the waist with realistic creasing and weight.
Polished dark leather boots or minimalist sneakers (no logos), understated and contemporary.
One slim signet ring only — no additional accessories.

POSE & MOOD

He is seated upright on the giant bird’s back, shoulders relaxed, posture confident yet calm. Chin gently elevated.
Expression is serene and self-assured, eyes gazing toward the horizon.
The T-shirt and denim move subtly with the breeze, natural fabric motion.

LIGHTING (GOLDEN HOUR)

Warm late-afternoon sunlight (~6000K) coming from camera-left/back, creating gentle rim highlights along his face, clothing edges, and the bird’s feathers.
Soft fill light from the opposite side keeps skin fully natural and realistic.
Colors are rich but never oversaturated.

CAMERA / OPTICS / DOF

Shot on a real full-frame camera.
50mm lens at f/2.8, ISO 100–200, shutter speed 1/500–1/1000s to freeze subtle feather motion.
Medium depth of field: subject and nearby feathers sharp, distant hills and far flowers softly blurred.
Vertical composition with a low horizon to emphasize the sky.
An elegant S-curve formed by the bird’s tail guides the viewer’s eye through the frame.

STYLE & OUTPUT

Pinterest-style cinematic editorial grading.
Ultra-photorealistic, grounded fantasy realism.
8K resolution.
```

### 98. 穿红色缎面连衣裙，带身份锁的镜子自拍

Blurred kitchen background, shallow depth of field, realistic skin textures, and warm indoor lighting."

### 137. 电影般雨中湖畔情侣场景提示（参考锁定）

**Author**: [Özge](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-07  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的电影剧照，描绘一对浪漫情侣在雨中站在黑暗湖泊旁的木码头上。此提示需要上传一张参考图片，以严格锁定构图、氛围、光线和调色板，并着重表现湿润织物和雨水倒影等自然物理效果。

![电影般雨中湖畔情侣场景提示（参考锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767966111448_7r0ptm_G-FQtT3WUAAdYEY.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photoreal_cinematic_couple_rain_lakeside_close_frame",
      "version": "v1.2_LAKESIDE_RAIN_CLOSE_INTIMATE_EN",
      "priority": "highest"
    },
    "references": {
      "reference_image_1": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE (REQUIRED)",
        "purpose": "COMPOSITION_MOOD_LIGHTING_LOCK",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "preserve_pose_relationship": true,
        "preserve_weather_mood": true,
        "preserve_color_palette": true
      }
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "ultra_photoreal_cinematic_film_still",
      "sharpness": "natural_subject_focus",
      "film_grain": "subtle_35mm_film_grain",
      "color_grade": "moody_green_warm_film",
      "dynamic_range": "high",
      "skin_tone": "natural_true_to_life"
```

### 154. 超逼真镜面自拍提示词，具有详细的材质物理特性和身份锁定功能

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的图像生成提示，旨在创建极其逼真、原始、高对比度的镜面自拍。它指定了严格的身份锁定、皮肤纹理的生物保真度（TrueLens 物理）、精确的服装材质真实感（真空紧身平纹针织），以及环境细节，如逼真的镜面瑕疵和清晰的背景，旨在营造一种未经编辑的社交媒体分享美学。

![超逼真镜面自拍提示词，具有详细的材质物理特性和身份锁定功能](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767803990935_pssts9_G-BFr8xXcAEt6Xw.jpg)

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast mirror selfie captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from the ornate mirror frame to the wooden textures in the background.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, a natural "satin-finish" glow, and fine peach fuzz catching the light ONLY along the jawline.
```

```
Top Left: She blows artificial snow from her palms towards the camera.
Bottom Left: She holds glowing fairy lights and a red bauble, smiling warmly.
Top Right: She leans on the box edge, holding a wine bottle, pouring red wine downwards so the liquid stream exits the bottom of this frame.
```

### 167. 80 年代一次性相机生日肖像，带身份锁

**Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-22  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，用于生成具有强烈 20 世纪 80 年代一次性相机美学风格的超现实肖像。它要求严格保留上传图像中的身份，将主体置于花园露台上，手持香烟，旁边有一张塑料桌，上面摆放着复古物品（Walkman、Game Boy、带点燃蜡烛的蛋糕）。关键技术特征是刺眼的正面直射闪光灯和厚重的胶片颗粒感。

![80 年代一次性相机生日肖像，带身份锁](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667286143_x8y2sb_G8vpW0_akAApcAC.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "hyper-realistic with strong 1980s nostalgia, disposable camera aesthetic",
  "resolution": "high-resolution (photorealistic base with vintage degradation)",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_uploaded_image": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "notes": "The woman’s face, facial structure, proportions, skin tone, and expression must remain 100% identical to the attached reference image. No facial alteration is allowed."
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "medium shot, seated",
    "camera_angle": "eye-level",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "pose": {
      "position": "sitting on a house garden deck",
      "interaction": "seated in front of a plastic garden table",
      "hands": {
        "right_or_left": "holding a cigarette casually",
        "gesture": "relaxed, natural"
      }
    },
    "expression": "calm, casual, slightly introspective",
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "blue tank top",
      "headwear": "none"
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "house garden deck",
    "surface": "wooden or composite deck flooring",
    "table": {
      "type": "simple plastic garden table",
      "objects_on_table": [
        {
          "item": "slice of cake",
          "details": "cake topped with many lit candles"
        },
        {
          "item": "Sony Walkman",
          "details": "classic cassette Walkman with wired headset resting beside it"
        },
        {
          "item": "Nintendo Game Boy",
          "details": "classic gray Game Boy with a Tetris cartridge placed next to it"
        },
        {
          "item": "ashtray",
          "details": "used ashtray with cigarette ash"
        }
      ]
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "direct camera flash",
    "style": "strong flash exposure",
    "effects": [
      "harsh frontal light",
      "flattened shadows",
      "slightly overexposed highlights"
    ]
  },
  "color_and_texture": {
    "contrast": "low contrast",
    "grain": "heavy film grain",
    "look": "80s disposable camera nostalgia",
    "tone": "washed colors with slight warmth"
  },
  "camera_style": {
    "inspiration": "1980s disposable point-and-shoot camera",
    "effects": [
      "visible flash glare",
      "minor color bleeding",
      "soft focus edges"
    ]
  },
  "mood": {
    "atmosphere": "nostalgic, intimate, retro",
    "emotion": "casual, reflective, everyday realism"
  },
  "quality_constraints": [
    "No modern digital look",
    "No AI-artifacts",
    "No watermarks or logos",
    "Preserve realistic proportions and lighting consistency"
  ],
  "output_goal": "Create a hyper-realistic yet nostalgically degraded 1980s-style photograph of a woman sitting on a garden deck in front of a plastic table with retro objects, cigarette in hand, strong flash light"
```

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBananaPro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid",
      "version": "v1.0",
      "priority": "high"
    },

        "type": "2x2_grid",
        "border": "thin_cream_gutter",
        "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_outfit_same_field"
      },
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "analog_film_kodak_portra_400"
    },
    "reference_constraints": {
      "character_reference_image": "UPLOAD_REF_IMAGE",
      "use_reference_face_only": true,
      "identity_lock": true,
      "strict_face_match": true,
      "preserve_facial_structure": true,
      "preserve_skin_tone": true,
      "preserve_hair": true,
      "no_face_mixing": true,
      "no_extra_people": true
    },
    "global_prompt": {
      "scene": "Tall grass field during golden hour sunset. Warm lens flares, dust motes dancing in light. A checkered picnic blanket is visible. Dreamy, romantic, soft focus atmosphere.",
      "subject": {
        "type": "young adult woman",
        "identity": "same person as reference image",
        "hair": "loose waves with a silk ribbon tied in a half-up style",
        "makeup": "no-makeup makeup look, sun-kissed freckles, flushed cheeks",
        "outfit": "white linen milkmaid dress with puffy sleeves and corset detail, bare feet",
        "prop": "vintage hardcover book and a green apple"
      },
      "camera": {
        "capture": "analog film",
        "lens_equivalent": "50mm",
        "focus": "soft focus",
        "depth_of_field": "medium"
      }
    },
    "frames": [
      {
        "frame_id": "A",
        "position": "top_left",
        "shot_type": "high_angle_looking_down",
        "pose": "Lying on back on the picnic blanket, holding the book above face to block the sun, hair spread out.",
        "expression": "playful, laughing"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "B",
        "position": "top_right",
        "shot_type": "seated_profile",
        "pose": "Sitting cross-legged, biting into the green apple, looking toward the sunset horizon.",
        "expression": "peaceful, content"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "C",
        "position": "bottom_left",
        "shot_type": "waist_up",
        "pose": "Walking through the tall grass, hands brushing the tops of the wheat, looking back at camera.",
        "expression": "inviting, candid"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "D",
        "position": "bottom_right",
        "shot_type": "macro_detail",

        "expression": "focused reading"
      }
    ]
  }
```

```
{
```

```
      ],

        "beauty_filter_face_change"
      ]

  },

    "goal": "Hyperrealistic winter night flash fashion portrait in a snowy pine forest",
    "meta": {
      "image_type": "Night Flash Portrait / Winter Fashion / Social Media Photo",
      "quality": "Ultra-HD, Hyperrealistic, High Detail",

    },

      "makeup": "soft glam, defined brows, nude lipstick, subtle highlight",
      "wardrobe": {
        "hat": "white fuzzy faux-fur hat",
        "dress": "white off-shoulder fitted cable-knit sweater dress, mini length",
        "wrists": "white fuzzy cuffs",

      },
      "accessories": "delicate necklace (optional, subtle)"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "snowy evergreen forest at night",
      "background": "dense snow-covered pine trees with dark teal/blue shadows",
      "weather": "active snowfall with visible snowflakes in foreground"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "night flash photography",

    },
```

### 171. 城市叛逆电影肖像提示（身份锁定）

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2025-12-21  **Language**: en

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "hyper-realistic, cinematic, urban rebel aesthetic",
  "resolution": "8K",
  "identity_preservation": {
    "use_reference_image": true,
    "strict_identity_lock": true,
    "alter_face": false,
    "notes": "Maintain the woman’s precise facial features, hairstyle, skin tone, body proportions, age, and expression with 100% accuracy based on the uploaded reference image."
```

### 175. 四格情绪网格生成器（喜悦、愤怒、悲伤、乐趣）

**Author**: [iX | AI Video Creator](https://x.com/iX00AI)  **Date**: 2025-12-21  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，用于自动生成一个四格构图（2x2 网格），展示一个一致的角色（基于上传的图片）表达四种不同的情绪：喜悦、愤怒、悲伤和乐趣。它为每个画面指定了摄像机角度、表情、肢体语言和灯光，同时保持了身份的一致性。

![四格情绪网格生成器（喜悦、愤怒、悲伤、乐趣）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489555568_61lo27_G8sVgUsaUAAX1L9.jpg)

```
Using the uploaded reference image, generate a four-panel composition (upper-left, upper-right, lower-left, lower-right).

Keep the person’s face, hairstyle, and clothing exactly the same as in the uploaded image for all panels.
Maintain a realistic photo style, consistent identity, and natural lighting.

Upper-left (Joy / 喜び):
A close-up of her face from a slightly high angle. She is smiling brightly with sparkling eyes, expressing pure joy and happiness. Her expression feels open, warm, and genuinely delighted.

Upper-right (Anger / 怒り):
A medium shot of her upper body. She is visibly angry, with furrowed brows and a sharp, intense expression. Her posture is tense, and she slightly clenches her fists or crosses her arms, clearly showing irritation or frustration.

Lower-left (Sadness / 哀しみ):
An over-the-shoulder or slightly downward-angled shot. Her body language is subdued and closed off. She looks down with a sorrowful, quiet expression, conveying loneliness or emotional pain, with a soft, muted mood.

Lower-right (Fun / 楽しい):
A casual selfie-style shot. She looks playful and energetic, laughing or making a cheerful, fun expression. The mood is lighthearted and carefree, showing her enjoying the moment.
```

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度描述性的提示，以生成一张具有电影剧照美学的超现实电影级照片。它要求严格保留参考照片中的面部相似度，描绘一位身穿皮草大衣的女士手持一杯红酒，以低角度自拍，背景是白雪皑皑的木制山区小屋。

![冬季电影感自拍提示词（身份锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489519282_zixfb8_G8rqML5bYAACEOt.jpg)
![冬季电影感自拍提示词（身份锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489519695_apjpvj_G8rqMKHbIAAYUan.jpg)

```
Create an ultra-realistic cinematic photograph in a film-still aesthetic, based strictly on the face from the provided reference photo, preserving 100% facial likeness with absolutely no changes to facial structure or hair.
The image is captured as a low-angle selfie, with the camera slightly tilted upward, creating a dynamic perspective that emphasizes the grandeur of a wooden mountain chalet in the background, its roof heavily covered in snow. The upper lines of the building recede into perspective, enhancing the dramatic low-angle composition.
The woman is framed in a tight close-up. Her face is subtly tilted forward toward the camera, making her facial features appear more expressive: full lips, a clearly defined jawline, and balanced proportions. Her expression is calm and confident, with a soft, sensual half-smile.
She is wearing a voluminous, natural fluffy fur coat that fills the lower part of the frame due to the shooting angle. In her hand—raised slightly higher than usual because of the selfie perspective—she holds a large glass of red wine close to the camera, creating an almost three-dimensional effect. The wine has a deep ruby tone with cinematic softness, and gold rings are visible on her fingers.
Her straight hair is lightly dusted with snowflakes. Above her head, the sky and the chalet roof are visible, both densely covered in snow. Large snowflakes drift slowly through the air, appearing in both the foreground and background, adding depth and atmosphere.
Film look characteristics:
soft film grain;
pastel, slightly muted color palette;
gentle highlights on the glass and hair;
warm skin tones contrasting with cool bluish-gray hues of the snow and sky;
subtle vignette around the corners;
35mm film effect: smooth light transitions, natural shadows, no digital sharpness;
fine dust and microscopic film imperfections (optional).
The overall atmosphere is aesthetic, luxurious, relaxed, and wintry, evoking the feeling of a living cinematic moment and true presence in the scene.
```

```
A powerful adult male fills the extreme foreground, lunging toward the camera with one arm fully extended, fingers reaching past the lens. His expression is pure survival panic — eyes wide, mouth open mid-scream. The face is razor-sharp, perfectly integrated, and emotionally intense.

Behind them, a massive stadium environment erupts. A violent explosion blossoms outward, throwing concrete, metal fragments, and dust into the air. > 一个复杂的 JSON 提示词，用于通过输入照片生成图像，旨在将美学风格转换为暖色调、复古、室内傍晚闪光肖像。至关重要的是，它包含严格的身份锁定规则，以确保主体面部与输入图像 100% 相同，同时应用特定的复古效果、逼真的皮肤纹理规则和详细的构图设置。
```

```
"Marble/stone console table with a floral arrangement.",
```

### 195. 2x2 网格角色一致性提示（JSON）

**Author**: [SDT🌿](https://x.com/SDT_side)  **Date**: 2025-12-20  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的 JSON 格式提示，旨在 2x2 网格布局的四个不同帧中保持上传参考图像的身份。场景聚焦于一位饥饿的日本女性，在公寓内的各种姿势和环境中被捕捉。

![2x2 网格角色一致性提示（JSON）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766386005027_m9m1zz_G8mHs5Ra0AAVMN-.jpg)

```
{
  "layout": {
    "type": "2x2 grid",
    "description": "画面を4等分した2×2構成。各フレームに同一人物を使用し、距離・構図・アングル・視点をすべて変える。"
  },
  "source": {
    "mode": "image_reference",
    "reference_images": {
      "primary": "base_person_image"
    },
    "preserve": {
      "same_person": true,
      "identity_lock": true,
      "keep_face": true,
      "keep_hairstyle": true,
      "keep_outfit": true
    }
  },
  "subject": {
    "person": "Japanese woman",
    "emotion": "hungry but playful, slightly tired, relatable"
  },
  "poses": {
    "variation_rule": "each frame uses a different composition and angle",
    "base_shot_type": "middle shot",
    "frame_variations": [
      "sitting at a small apartment table, shoulders slightly slumped, holding her stomach with one hand, faint amused smile",
      "leaning back in a chair, head tilted up, eyes half-closed, one hand resting on her stomach as if enduring hunger",
      "standing in the kitchen area, arms loosely crossed over her midsection, looking toward the fridge with a resigned playful expression",
      "sitting on the sofa, knees drawn slightly up, one hand pressing lightly on her stomach, soft laugh at her own situation"
    ]
  },
  "accessories": {
    "handheld_item": "empty plate or nothing in hands"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "small apartment interior",
    "room_type": "kitchen and living area",
    "time": "late afternoon",
    "context": "missed lunch, waiting until dinner",
    "details": [
      "simple dining table",
      "compact kitchen",
      "sofa and low table",
      "everyday lived-in apartment feel"
    ]
  },
  "lighting": {
    "primary": "soft natural daylight from window",
    "secondary": "subtle indoor ambient light"
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot_type": "middle shot",
    "lens_feel": "slight wide-angle",
    "framing": "waist-up, subject centered with gentle variation per frame"
  },
  "color_tone": "natural color, neutral skin tones, realistic indoor daylight balance",
  "image_quality": {
    "realism": "photorealistic",
    "style": "casual everyday snapshot"
  }
}
```

### 197. 运动健身房自拍身份保留提示词

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2025-12-20  **Language**: en

> 一个针对 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 的高度具体的提示，旨在生成一张年轻女性在健身房环境中拍摄的逼真、休闲健身自拍，并强调基于上传的参考图像 100% 保留身份。

```
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "{argument name="face identity" default="uploaded reference image"}",
      "identity_lock": {argument name="identity lock" default="true"},

    },

      "type": "{argument name="subject type" default="young woman"}",
      "expression": "{argument name="expression" default="soft relaxed expression with slightly glossy lips"}",
      "gaze": "{argument name="gaze" default="looking slightly past the camera with calm confidence"}",
      "pose": {
        "position": "{argument name="pose position" default="close-up selfie angle from slightly above"}",
        "head": "{argument name="head tilt" default="subtle tilt"}",
        "posture": "{argument name="posture" default="casual and natural"}"
      }
    },

    "hair": {
      "color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark brown"}",
      "style": "{argument name="hair style" default="pulled back into a low ponytail or tied-back style with clean hairline"}"
    },

    "makeup": {
      "style": "{argument name="makeup style" default="natural sporty glow"}",
      "details": [
        "{argument name="makeup detail 1" default="dewy skin finish"}",
        "{argument name="makeup detail 2" default="defined brows"}",
        "{argument name="makeup detail 3" default="light mascara"}",
        "{argument name="makeup detail 4" default="natural blush"}",
        "{argument name="makeup detail 5" default="soft glossy pink lips"}"
      ]
    },

    "outfit": {
      "top": "{argument name="top" default="loose white graphic t-shirt"}",

        "{argument name="accessory 1" default="white over-ear headphones resting around the neck"}",
        "{argument name="accessory 2" default="small stud earrings"}"
      ]
    },

    "environment": {

        "{argument name="background element 1" default="gym benches"}",
        "{argument name="background element 2" default="exercise machines"}",
        "{argument name="background element 3" default="wooden floor"}",
        "{argument name="background element 4" default="soft daylight coming through windows"}"
      ]
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "{argument name="lighting type" default="natural gym lighting"}",

        "{argument name="lighting characteristic 1" default="soft highlights on skin"}",

      ]
    },

      "depth_of_field": "{argument name="depth of field" default="shallow with background slightly blurred"}",
      "mood": "{argument name="mood" default="fresh, sporty, effortless"}"
    },

    "render_quality": {
```

### 198. 花卉咖啡馆里的仙女风镜面自拍（结构化）

**Author**: [Javeriya ✨](https://x.com/JadoonKhan281)  **Date**: 2025-12-20  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，可能采用自定义格式（非纯 JSON），用于生成一张在浪漫花卉咖啡馆中的全身镜面自拍。它要求严格遵循参考照片中人物的身份、发型和表情，并详细描述了淡粉色紧身胸衣连衣裙、蝴蝶高跟鞋以及舒适的咖啡馆环境。

![花卉咖啡馆里的仙女风镜面自拍（结构化）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385983689_gbfcp7_G8lGMpjXQAANVqI.jpg)

```
[subject]
reference_adherence = Strictly match the provided reference photo face exactly
hair = black
hairstyle = exact hairstyle from reference
makeup = Natural style as per reference
expression = Soft, calm, looking at phone screen

[subject.facial_features]
0 = Preserve exact face shape
1 = Match eye structure and eyebrow shape
2 = Retain lip shape and natural color

[apparel]
main_garment = Soft pastel pink, romantic corset-style mini dress inspired by a fairy-core aesthetic. Off-shoulder neckline with delicate gathered fabric, lace-up corset bodice that cinches the waist, and a flowy chiffon skirt with layered movement. Long, sheer, flared sleeves that drape gracefully with light fabric transparency. Dress matches exactly the reference pink dress in color, silhouette, and romantic style.
fabric_physics = Lightweight chiffon and satin blend, airy movement, natural folds, soft wind-like flow
footwear = Pastel blush pink satin high-heeled sandals with a square toe. Delicate thin straps adorned with embroidered 3D butterfly appliqués across the front and ankle straps. Slim feminine heel, elegant fairy-core aesthetic, matching exactly the reference butterfly heels in color, texture, and romantic detail.

[apparel.accessories]
0 = Silver necklace
1 = Silver bracelet
2 = Silver rings

[pose_and_action]
type = Full-body mirror selfie
stance = Squatting low gracefully, one knee forward, leaning slightly toward mirror
head_position = Tilted slightly downward
props = Smartphone with soft pink phone case, soft pastel tone, minimal design

[pose_and_action.hands]
right_hand = Holding phone vertically in front of face
left_hand = Resting gently on knee

[environment]
location = Charming floral cafe interior
background = Romantic European-style floral cafe with stone-textured walls, hanging wicker baskets, dried flower arrangements, pastel floral bouquets, vintage wooden shelves, rustic beams, and soft decorative mirrors. Warm neutral stone tones mixed with soft pinks, greens, creams, and lavender florals. Cozy, aesthetic, feminine atmosphere.
flooring = Vintage patterned tile floor with subtle reflections

[lighting_and_atmosphere]
quality = Soft, ambient cafe lighting with gentle highlights
mood = Feminine, romantic, elegant, fairy-core, social media aesthetic

[technical_specifications]
quality = 8K resolution, photorealistic, high fidelity
focus = Sharp focus on face and outfit
perspective = Eye-level mirror perspective
aspect_ratio = 4:5

[negative_prompt]
0 = Incorrect face
1 = Wrong hairstyle
2 = Extra limbs
3 = Distorted proportions
4 = Different dress color or style
5 = Different shoes
6 = Text
7 = Watermark
8 = Blurry
9 = Low resolution
10 = Artificial looking skin
```
